\section{ilpTest1}

\[\begin{array}{c| c c@{\hskip 2pt} c@{\hskip 2pt} }

\end{array}\]
No initialization required \ $\rightarrow$\  Proceed to Optimize

\[\begin{array}{c| c c@{\hskip 2pt} c@{\hskip 2pt} }

\end{array}\]

\[\begin{array}{c| c c@{\hskip 2pt} c@{\hskip 2pt} }

\end{array}\]

\[\begin{array}{c| c c@{\hskip 2pt} c@{\hskip 2pt} c@{\hskip 2pt} }

\end{array}\]

\hline
z    &  -1 & -0.666667 y_{1} & -1 y_{2} & -2 y_{3}\\
\end{array}\]

\hline
z    &  1 & -1 x_{5} &   \\
